< Text>
called Monday for a acrylic fill appointment after basically all other nail salons being closed on Memorial Day. There was one man working and he told me to come back at 6pm. I arrived and he was still working on someone so I waited until 6:45pm. Not a big deal. Finally it was my turn and very rudely he told me to pick a color, I told him I wanted a light pink color. I also told him I wanted plan acrylic fill and a paint polish on top of the acrylic. I work at a hospital and gel, poly gel, dip powder all reacts with the chemicals and comes off.

He argued with me telling me he couldn't and questioning what I wanted. I finally told him I just wanted my nails done, I told him I wanted glitter at the tips and he also ignored what I wanted.
Every time I asked him a question he ignored it like I was an inconvenience and he wanted to go home. Ag this point I was irritated and decided I would do my own glitter and file at home.

He did not file my nails and did a poor job,
When he was done he asked if I would pay cash or card, I told him card. I also told him I needed to wait a few minutes for my nails to dry before I reached in my pocket and got my bank card. When I go to pay there is a large sign at the counter stating "all tips on cash only" the man takes my bank card and started screaming how much would I like to top because he can add it on. I said sir the sign says tip in cash I can get cash from my car. He asked where my car was and wanted to follow me.
Save yourself and take your business elsewhere.</Text>

<name>K Lauderdale< /name>< review>
Large thrift store. Staff are present, generally polite but would not consider them friendly. This thrift store sells loads of clothing, books, CDs, dishes, furniture, small appliances, and some plant/gardening things.  Store is a bit grubby so bring some hand sanitize. Dishes and clothing are jam packed in the place to the point that it makes it difficult to shop and pick things up as there are way to many items all stuffed together. Did pick up a couple of items but generally they seem to be a bit overpriced on many of the items. However, not the worst thrift store I have come across and would consider going again.< /review>

Came here for a service on my A4. I was able to hear a rattling noise from the right side of my dash which was very tough to reproduce. My advisor was David de Latore.
